#第一阶段：八省战争

	### 起义开始 ###
	country_event = {
		id = CHI.earlygame.000
		immediate = { 
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event CHI.earlygame.000" 
			set_country_flag = CHI_phase_one_begins_flag
		}
		title = CHI.earlygame.000.t
		desc = CHI.earlygame.000.d
		picture = GFX_report_event_CHI_warlord_battle

		is_triggered_only = yes #Fired from Lepcollapse.18
		option = { #Fu Zhan!
			name = CHI.earlygame.000.a
			add_war_support = 0.05
			add_political_power = 60
		}
	}

	### 1936年的农忙 ###
	country_event = {
		id = CHI.earlygame.001
		immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event CHI.earlygame.001" }
		title = CHI.earlygame.001.t
		desc = CHI.earlygame.001.d
		picture = GFX_report_event_CHI_economic

		is_triggered_only = yes #Triggered by CHI.earlygame.000, should be on June 24th, 1936

		option = { #They'll have to get used to these changes for the greater good.
			name = CHI.earlygame.001.a
			ai_chance = { base = 50 }
			add_command_power = 30
			add_stability = -0.10
			CHI_add_rad_small_effect = yes
		}

		option = { #Divert new recruits to get some moral training in the fields.
			name = CHI.earlygame.001.b
			ai_chance = { base = 50 }
			add_manpower = -5000
			add_political_power = 50
			add_war_support = 0.05
		}
	}

	### 请求欧洲援助 ###	
	country_event = { # get support from europe
		id = CHI.earlygame.004
		immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event CHI.earlygame.004" }
		title = CHI.earlygame.004.t
		desc = CHI.earlygame.004.d
		picture = GFX_report_event_IRE_german_volunteers
		is_triggered_only = yes

		option = { # advisors and guns
			name = CHI.earlygame.004.a
			ai_chance = { base = 30 }
			add_political_power = -50
			CHI = {
				effect_tooltip = {
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = infantry_equipment
						amount = 500
						producer = ROOT
					}
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = artillery_equipment
						amount = 50
						producer = ROOT
					}
					add_opinion_modifier = {
						target = PREV
						modifier = KR_approves_of_govt
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = CHI.earlygame.5 days = 3 } #Event to CHI letting them know advisors and guns are on the way
			}
		}

		option = { # Solidarity but not for you
			name = CHI.earlygame.004.b
			ai_chance = {
				base = 20
				modifier = {
					add = -20
					OR = {
						tag = ENG
						tag = FRA
					}
				}
			}
			CHI = {
				effect_tooltip = {
					add_opinion_modifier = {
						target = PREV
						modifier = KR_disapproves_of_govt
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = CHI.earlygame.006 days = 3 } #Nothing
			}
		}
	}

	### 拿到欧洲援助 ###

				25 = {
					add_offsite_building = {
						type = arms_factory
						level = 1
					}
				}
				25 = {
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = infantry_equipment
						amount = 500
						producer = FROM
					}
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = artillery_equipment
						amount = 50
						producer = FROM
					}
				}
				50 = {
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = infantry_equipment
						amount = 500
						producer = FROM
					}
				}
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = FROM
				modifier = KR_approves_of_govt
			}

	}

	### 中央委员会归来 ###
	country_event = {
		id = CHI.earlygame.18
		immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event CHI.earlygame.18 FROM = [From.GetName]" }

		title = CHI.earlygame.018.t
		desc = {
			text = CHI.earlygame.018.d1
			trigger = {
				has_full_control_of_state = 803 # Wenzhou
			}
		}
		desc = {
			text = CHI.earlygame.018.d2
			trigger = {
				has_full_control_of_state = 802 # Xiamen
				NOT = { has_full_control_of_state = 803 } # Wenzhou
			}
		}
		desc = {
			text = CHI.earlygame.018.d3
			trigger = {
				NOT = { has_full_control_of_state = 803 } # Wenzhou
				NOT = { has_full_control_of_state = 802 } # Xiamen
			}
		}
		picture = GFX_report_event_FNG_protest

		is_triggered_only = yes
		fire_only_once = yes

		option = {
			name = CHI.earlygame.018.a
			custom_effect_tooltip = CHI_krevent1_tt
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = infantry_equipment_0
				amount = 500
				producer = FRA
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = CHI_Mao_zedong_hog_tot
				add_idea = CHI_Liao_Zhongkai_hog_rso
			}
			CHI_RCA_medium_effect = yes
			hidden_effect = {
				random_controlled_state = {
					prioritize = { 802 803 1046 }
					create_unit = {
						owner = ROOT
						division = "name = \"Committee's Own\" division_template = \"Zhenggui Shih\" start_experience_factor = 0.5 start_equipment_factor = 1.0 force_equipment_variants = { infantry_equipment_1 = { owner = FRA } artillery_equipment_1 = { owner = FRA } }"
					}
				}
				add_country_leader_role = {
					character = CHI_committee
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						ideology = radsoc_tridemism_subtype
						expire = "1965.1.1.1"
						desc = CHI_committee_desc
						traits = {
							CHI_struggle_of_line
						}
					}
				}
				clr_country_flag = Li_Shiqun_dead
				clr_country_flag = Gu_Zhenggang_dead

		}

	### 弹劾投票 ###
	country_event = { #The Impeachment Vote
		id = CHI.lategame.021
		immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event CHI.lategame.021" }
		title = CHI.lategame.021.t
		desc = CHI.lategame.021.d
		picture = GFX_report_event_CHI_song_qingling_speech_party_conference_2
	
		is_triggered_only = yes #Triggered by focus CHI_third_national_congress
	
		option = { #The die is cast...
			name = CHI.lategame.021.a
			custom_effect_tooltip = CHI_impeachment_tt
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_game_rule = { rule = CHI_PATH option = DEFAULT }
						is_ai = no
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						power_balance_value = {
							id = CHI_power_balance
							value > 0
						}
					}
					hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = CHI.lategame.022 days = 1 } } #Wang is ousted from power!
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						power_balance_value = {
							id = CHI_power_balance
							value < 0
						}
					}
					hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = CHI.lategame.025 days = 1 } } #Wang Carries the Day!
				}
				else = {
					hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = CHI.lategame.022 days = 1 } } 
				}
			}
			else = {
				#Cheaty, cheaty gamerules
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_game_rule = { rule = CHI_PATH option = CHI_PATH_JINGWEI_RADSOC }
					}
					hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = CHI.lategame.022 days = 1 } } #Chaos on the Convention Floor
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_game_rule = { rule = CHI_PATH option = CHI_PATH_QINGLING_RADSOC }
					}
					hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = CHI.lategame.025 days = 1 } } #Wang is ousted from power!
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				set_country_flag = CHI_red_star_shines_over_China
				mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
				remove_power_balance = { id = CHI_power_balance }
				country_event = { id = CHI.lategame.028 days = 30 random_days = 15 }
			}
		}
	}

country_event = {
	id = CHI.lategame.1067
	title = CHI.lategame.1067.t
	desc = CHI.lategame.1067.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CHI_CRS_officers

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = CHI.lategame.1067.a
		remove_ideas = CHI_mdjh_idea
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = totalist
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		CHI_hu_zongnan = {
			promote_character = totalist_tridemism_subtype
			set_portraits = {
				army = { large = "gfx/leaders/CHI/CHI_Hu_Zongnan_WYZ.png" }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			CHI_dai_chunfeng = { promote_character = authoritarian_democrat_subtype }
			CHI_lixingshe = { promote_character = paternal_autocrat_subtype }
		}
		activate_advisor = CHI_lixingshe_sic
		add_popularity = { ideology = totalist popularity = 0.20 }

		#Fallback to ensure everything works properly character-wise
		CHI_retire_LCS_advisors_effect = yes
		CHI_retire_PAC_endgame_advisors_effect = yes
		CHI_retire_RCA_endgame_advisors_effect = yes
		CHI_retire_LCS_generals_effect = yes
		CHI_retire_PAC_generals_effect = yes
		CHI_retire_RCA_generals_effect = yes
		CHI_recruit_CRS_generals_effect = yes
		CHI_recruit_CRS_endgame_advisors_effect = yes
		CHI_recruit_RCF_generals_effect = yes
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
		complete_national_focus = CHI_the_second_national_revolution
	}
}
